Provincial Order to Ban Competitive Sales by Stores

Discounted competitive sales by stores are actually an improper act by merchants. The government, in view of this, has already banned and prohibited it. However, the stores in this city, whenever business is slow, use price reductions as a gimmick, disregarding the ban. In addition, since the beginning of autumn, some use the completion of a new house as a gimmick, some use the anniversary of one week to even twenty or thirty weeks as a gimmick, some use adding _ adding five to buy one foot and giving one foot as a gimmick, and even giving away gifts. In fact, they secretly increase the price, which is a kind of deceptive behavior towards customers and is not the way of trade. It is also heard that the provincial government has issued an order to the county, ordering the Chamber of Commerce and the Public Security Bureau to immediately implement a ban, prohibiting any more competitive sales behavior.

Special Article

Discussion on the Construction Procedures of the Huai River Diversion Project into the Sea in Jiangsu Province - Lan Xianjun

The harm caused by the Huai River in our country has been a long time coming. The three provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, and Henan often have the worry of the Huai River flooding their fields and houses, especially Subei at the tail end, which suffers the most. The great flood of the 20th year of the Republic inundated more than ten counties along the _ River, turning them into a country of Ze. The huge loss was no less than tens of millions of yuan, because the Huai River invaded the _ Canal. Therefore, the Huai River Diversion Association is actively preparing for the implementation of the Huai River Diversion. The planned diversion of the Huai River is based on the principle of separating the river from the sea, and the sea route still takes the path of the abandoned Yellow River, in order to ensure safety and reduce resistance. However, the first phase of the project requires 16 million yuan, which is deeply felt to be difficult to organize. In order to achieve this as soon as possible, Jiangsu Province tried its best to raise funds and cooperate with the Huai River Diversion Association, and implemented the conscription according to the method of dredging the Liutang River, which shows the spirit of cooperation between the officials and people of Jiangsu, and the good plan of the long-term officials to benefit the people and eliminate harm. Once the Huai River enters the sea and the waterway is completed, the flood of Subei can be reduced, and the poverty of the people's livelihood can be changed, which is not the beginning of the happiness of our people. However, this project is huge, starting from Yangzhuang in Huaiyin to Taozikou, with a total length of about 170 to 80 kilometers, and about 60 to 70 million cubic meters of earth being excavated. The provincial government plans to handle it in two years, with 3 million yuan to be raised each year and more than 100,000 workers. In two years, the Huai River entering the sea project will be fully completed, and its planning is thorough, and the legal meaning is good, which is enough to be praised. However, yesterday I read in the newspaper that the Huai River entering the sea project is planned to gradually dredge eastward from Yangzhuang, and the beach cutting project from Qitao to Taozikou will be held in the second phase. I was surprised to hear this, and I did not dare to be shy and humbly put forward which Huai River project should be done first and which should be done later, hoping that the authorities will look into it.

Since the merger of the Huai and Yellow Rivers, the Yellow sand has been deposited, and floods have occurred from time to time. Since the Yellow River changed its course, the river has become increasingly silted up, but the current river is slightly lower in the eastern section than in the west. According to the measurements of the Huai River Diversion Association over the years, this is also the case. The road from Qitao to Yuhuangkou is long and difficult to dredge. It is better to cut the beach from Qitao to Taozikou, which is less expensive than entering the sea along the old road, and the water flow must be smooth. The Huai River Diversion Association plans to cut the beach from this section, which has a reason. According to the Huai River entering the sea project, it is 170 to 80 kilometers away. According to the terrain, it is more appropriate to first cut the beach to dredge the sea waterway. The provincial government's pre-scheduled plan is to complete the embankment of 80 to 90 kilometers in one year of construction. If the lower section is constructed, the river from Beisha to Taozikou will be unobstructed and unimpeded in one year. If so, the rainwater along the Yellow River in Huaihuai Lianfu will have no fear of stopping and storing, and even the great flood of the 20th year of the Republic will not overflow and cause disaster, and the danger of affecting the _ Canal can be reduced. Moreover, the millions of people along the Yellow River below Yangzhuang can be spared the fear of being submerged. If not, if the upper section is dredged, before the entire project is completed, it will not be possible to divert the water of the Huai River and inject it into the present. The river that is planned to be dredged will become a broken alley and an abandoned port. It cannot divert water or drain water. It is a waste. It must wait until the entire sea project is completed before its effect can be realized. In case of autumn floods, _ rain is a disaster. Now the unfinished river will be the confluence of four waters. The upper water cannot be blocked and the dyke will be breached and go downstream. The lower water cannot be blocked and not caused by a flood, then the flood of several counties along the coast will not only not be reduced compared to the past but also exceed it. If the authorities think about this, they will not invert the procedures and dredge from Yangzhuang. If the upper section is repaired, the effect of water conservancy will not be seen, but the real cellar has arrived, and the tragedy of the great flood of the 20th year of the Republic can be easily reproduced in the eyes of the people in several counties along the Yellow River. Therefore, I am familiar with the weight of the interests and gains and losses. This diversion of the Huai River into the sea project should be more appropriate to start construction from the lower section.

The area of wasteland in Subei is 8,100 square kilometers, which is about 13 million mu. However, the current economic strength of Jiangsu Province cannot fully carry out reclamation. Therefore, the provincial government decided to proceed in stages, dividing the area north of Jiaoxie to south of Xinyang Port as the first phase of the project, and the area north of Xinyang Port to south of Chenjiagang as the second phase of the project. However, only 6.35 million mu are reclaimed in the first phase, and the other vast and good soil wasteland will be left to the future, which is a pity. However, the wasteland from north of Xinyang Port to south of Chenjiagang accounts for more than two-thirds in the Huai River basin. This time, Jiangsu Province is working hard to assist in the diversion of the Huai River, which is not only enthusiastic about national construction but also has a huge relationship with itself. Last year, the Huai River Diversion Association estimated that after the completion of the Huai River Diversion project, Jiangsu Province can increase the production of 17 million dan of rice and 46 million dan of wheat every year. Although this is calculated based on the tributaries of the Huai River in Jiangsu Province and within its basin, the scope of its sea basin actually accounts for the majority. This vast _ land can be of great benefit to the people's livelihood, but the water conservancy project has not been carried out, and millions of acres of arable land have been turned into wasteland, causing the coastal people to be surplus and unable to make a living, or fleeing to the south of the Yangtze River, or even becoming bandits, affecting society, which is not insignificant. Therefore, it should be remedied urgently. Now Jiangsu Province is working hard to assist the Huai River Diversion Association, and imitating the example of dredging the Liutang River, conscripting labor and implementing the project, hoping to turn the wasteland into mature soil as soon as possible, which is very obvious. If the provincial government takes into account the overall situation, changes the intended meaning of the pre-scheduled Huai River entering the sea project, it may as well implement the project in the lower section. It can not only be said to the people of Jiangsu that the progress of wasteland reclamation in Subei should start from the scope of the second phase, but also avoid the delay of leaving the wasteland to the reclamation of the second phase. However, although it cannot be compared with the wasteland reclamation in the first phase, it can also make up for the shortcomings, which is not a small amount. Wouldn't it be beneficial to both the national economy and the people's livelihood?

Now, Jiangsu Province's diversion of the Huai River into the sea is said to be assisting the Huai River Diversion Association, but in fact, it is only based on the plans measured by the Huai River Diversion Association over the years, and the conscription and fundraising are all the responsibility of the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Therefore, its construction procedures are also determined by its own weighing and handling, which is completely incomparable to those who rely on others. All things in the world cannot have both advantages and disadvantages. There must be harm in having advantages. If you can avoid harm and take advantage, then you will get it. Moreover, diverting the Huai River from the lower section not only has no harm in harming your neighbors but also has the benefit of reclaiming wasteland. Therefore, I dare not spare the cost of words and urge the authorities to act expediently and change the construction procedures of the Huai River diversion. What is the first result of my ignorance? I don't know what the high-minded people think.

The Yuping Railway Loan Agreement Was Signed Yesterday

The agreement includes two parts: a mortgage loan and materials.

The total amount of 16 million is underwritten by the Shanghai Banking Consortium.

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company officially signed the loan agreement with the lending banks yesterday at 11:00 AM in the conference room on the second floor of the Bank of China. The agreement consists of two parts: one for 8 million between the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company and the lending banking consortium, and the other for 8 million between the consortium and the German Otto Wolff Materials Factory, totaling 16 million yuan. The company will submit the agreement to the Ministry of Railways and then to the Executive Yuan for record-keeping. Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction, arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou yesterday to oversee everything. The details are as follows:

Negotiation Process

In order to build the Yuping Railway, the Ministry of Railways and the governments of Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces used the first phase of railway construction bonds and Yuping Road bonds, each worth 12 million yuan, to obtain a mortgage loan of 8 million yuan from banks such as the Bank of China in Shanghai, and a mortgage loan of 8 million yuan from the German Otto Wolff Materials Factory, totaling 16 million yuan. The mortgage loan from the German materials factory was signed on behalf of the lending consortium, which also kept all the mortgaged bonds in its custody. As for the loan agreement, the Ministry of Railways and the governments of Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces reviewed and revised the contract terms with the lending banks at the Bank of China in Shanghai on September 25. It was originally planned that the agreement could be signed immediately, but the signing was delayed until now due to negotiations with the German materials factory on the price of materials.

Convening a Meeting

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company, having resolved the issue of material prices, convened a formal signing conference at 12:00 noon yesterday in the conference room on the second floor of the Bank of China on the Bund, inviting the lending banks to attend. Those present included Zeng Yangfu, Chairman of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company; Zhang Gongquan and Huo Baoshu of the Bank of China; Xu Xinliu of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; Wu Yunzhai of the Jincheng Bank; Wang Zhixin of the Xinhua Bank; Xu Boyuan of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau; and Dr. Bick of the German Otto Wolff Materials Factory, among others, more than ten people in total. Zeng Yangfu first checked the full text of the contract item by item, and then the representatives of the banks formally signed the contract. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 PM.

Signing Representatives

There were two contracts signed yesterday: (1) Between the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company and the lending banks, signed by Zeng Yangfu, Chairman of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company; Zhang Gongquan of the Bank of China representing the banking consortium; Xu Xinliu of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; Yang Jimei of the Shanghai Bank; Wu Yunzhai of the Jincheng Bank; Wang Zhixin of the Xinhua Bank; Xu Boyuan of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau; and Zeng Yangfu of the Zhejiang Provincial Government. Wu Jiantao, representative of the Jiangxi Provincial Government and the Jiangxi Yumin Bank, was absent and will sign later. (2) Between the banking consortium and the German Otto Wolff Materials Factory, signed by Zhang Gongquan representing the banking consortium and Dr. Bick representing the Otto Wolff Factory. Attached to the mortgage materials loan agreement was a material purchase agreement between the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company and the Otto Wolff Factory. This agreement specifically stipulated the types and prices of materials required and when they should be delivered. It was also signed yesterday by Zeng Yangfu and Dr. Bick.

Agreement Content

The agreement signed between the banking consortium and the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Company amounted to 8 million, with an interest rate of 1% and a repayment period of four and a half years. The mortgage material loan agreement also amounted to 8 million, with an interest rate of 0.7% and a repayment period of five and a half years. Interest will start accruing after the materials are shipped to China. The attached material purchase agreement fully specifies the types and prices of materials required and the dates for phased shipments to China. As for the method of repaying principal and interest, when the first phase of railway construction bonds and Yuping Railway bonds are drawn for redemption, the banking consortium will collect and save all the principal and interest corresponding to the winning numbers and distribute them to the respective banks. Any remaining amount will be returned to the government, as the banking consortium is responsible for keeping all the bonds in custody. After the above agreements are sent to the representatives of the Jiangxi Provincial Government and the Jiangxi Yumin Bank for signing, the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company will submit them to the Ministry of Railways and then to the Executive Yuan for record-keeping.

Lending Banks

The loan was underwritten by a banking consortium organized by seven banks, including the Bank of China. The amount underwritten by each bank is as follows: Bank of China 3.75 million, Jincheng 1.5 million, Shanghai 1 million, Zhejiang Industrial 500,000, Xinhua 500,000, Jiangxi Yumin 500,000, and Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau 250,000, totaling 8 million yuan. The office of the banking consortium is located in the Bank of China.

Shipping Materials by Telegraph

This is the first time that the German Otto Wolff Factory has promoted its materials in China. The prices of various materials offered were negotiated and decided by the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company with the factory representative several times, based on the standard prices of the Construction Committee's material purchasing committee. Therefore, the prices of various materials are cheaper than those of other countries. The factory also believes that China's construction industry is booming and expects that there will be many transactions between the two sides in the future, so it is happy to accept the lowest price offered by our country. Dr. Bick, the representative of the factory, reported the signing process to the German factory by telegraph yesterday after the contract was signed and instructed them to ship the first batch of materials to China as soon as possible for application.

Recent Projects

The Xin Xin News Agency reporter learned from the Bank of China yesterday that the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway United Company had previously withdrawn more than 100,000 yuan from the Bank of China for surveying and excavation projects, which will be deducted from the loan in the future. Therefore, the Yuping Road project is progressing actively. The third section of the Yu-Nan section and the bridge project in Dongxiang and Jinxian are currently underway, and bids are being invited for construction. Once the German steel rails and sleepers are shipped to China, they can be laid.

China National Aviation Corporation's Stinson Aircraft Tested Blind Flying Yesterday

The two-hour flight yesterday morning yielded satisfactory results.

The Guangdong aircraft will test-fly Fuzhou at 8:00 AM this morning.

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, in order to ensure flight safety, China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) purchased blind flying equipment at a high price when ordering new aircraft from the United States. The equipment has been shipped to Shanghai with the new aircraft. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the equipment was installed on a Stinson aircraft and operated by a pilot recently sent to the United States to study blind flying. This experiment of flying an aircraft purely using scientific mechanical methods was the first in China. The aircraft took off from Longhua Airport at 9:00 AM. When it reached an altitude of 2,000 feet, the glass windows of the cockpit were covered with cloth. The direction, speed, and altitude were all determined by the blind flying instruments. Changes in weather pressure, wind force, and air thickness were recorded in detail at any time. The pilot only needed to control everything according to the instructions of the instruments. The blind flying test started at 9:00 AM and continued for two hours over Shanghai. At about 11:00 AM, it landed safely at Longhua Airport with satisfactory results. The two new aircraft prepared for the Shanghai-Guangdong route are equipped with this equipment. In the future, normal flights can be maintained even in dense fog or sudden weather changes.

Zhang Yichen's Letter to the Ratepayers' Association on Election Opinions

Using universal suffrage of citizens as the standard

Zhang Yichen and Zhang Xianfang, executive members of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Shanghai Public Concession, wrote to the association to solicit opinions on the election regulations. The letter stated, "We have received your letter and learned that your association is studying the election regulations and has organized a special committee and solicited opinions from various representatives, which shows that your association attaches great importance to the election. The Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association is a group of Chinese citizens in the concession and is the only organization for Chinese citizens' diplomacy, which is used to protect the rights of taxpayers in the concession. Its election is naturally limited to the qualification of paying taxes, which is very clear and there is no need for research. However, in the past elections, they were divided into groups such as the Tongxiang group, the business group, and the citizen group, etc., and the Tongxiang and business groups accounted for two-thirds of the number of representatives, which is not in accordance with the election law. Now that your association is improving the election regulations and putting forward research, it seems that it should be corrected to avoid malpractices. Because the members of these two groups are not only in the concession. For example, the Tongxiang Association and the Trade Association, regardless of Zhabei, the city, and the Chinese district, can join the Tongxiang Association if they are from the same hometown, and can join the Trade Association if they are in the same industry. Therefore, the members of these two groups are not limited by the Chinese concession and are composed of members with different addresses, which is not comparable to the citizen group in the concession. As for the election method, it is best to have genuine taxpayers in the concession elect half of the representatives through universal suffrage, and the other half should be elected from the candidates recommended by the citizen groups in the concession. The representatives produced by the two elections of the citizen universal suffrage group and the citizen group should periodically re-elect the Chinese directors, Chinese committee members, and executive members. If this method can be adopted, the procedures will be simpler, the nature will be consistent, and it will seem appropriate in terms of reason and law. The matter is related to the election administration and should be held legally. Since the election administration is important, it is even more related to the national system. We should put forward the above opinions and hope that your association will make a public decision to amend it for the convenience of the public."

The Municipal Party Headquarters Sent a Letter to the Municipal Government Requesting a Swift Resolution to Reduce Rents

And attached five opinions

The Municipal Party Headquarters of this city believes that reducing rents is an important strategy for prospering the market. After receiving a report from the First District Party Headquarters, it attached five opinions and sent a letter to the Municipal Government for review. The original text is recorded as follows: "The case is based on the report from the executive committee of the First District of the Municipal Council, which states that according to the report from the Twenty-seventh Branch, this city's people, due to the depression of all industries and economic bankruptcy in recent years, find it very difficult to maintain their lives. Therefore, house rent reduction committees have been organized everywhere in order to reduce the burden. As for the landlords, some voluntarily reduce rents in view of the depression, while most ignore the market situation and insist on not reducing rents, resulting in both parties going to extremes, disputes, and even fights and lawsuits, turning into tragedies. If this continues, there will be no peaceful days. In view of this, this branch submitted a resolution to the party members' general meeting, requesting the superiors to transfer the request to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government to quickly stipulate rent reduction regulations in order to follow and stop disputes. It is reasonable to record the case and request review, etc. Based on this, the 93rd regular meeting of the affiliated association passed the resolution to forward the case, etc. In view of this, reducing rents is indeed an important strategy for prospering the market, and rent reduction disputes will affect the progress of municipal administration. Therefore, this association has attached five opinions: (1) Rent reduction is very urgent, but if the Municipal Government sets a universal standard and forces both parties to comply, it is impossible in terms of law and fact. (2) The remedy is only that the tenants in a unit (such as tenants in the same alley or the same object) should unite by themselves and make a request to the landlord to reduce rents. (3) In the process of rent reduction negotiations, party and government agencies should allow tenants to organize temporary groups to handle negotiations. The Municipal Party Headquarters should also try to lead them. (4) When the landlord and tenant cannot reach an agreement, both parties or either party should request the rent dispute review committee of the Municipal Government to investigate the production price and mediate based on the facts within 20 days. However, the rent determined by the review committee should not be higher than the current rent. (5) The disputed landlord or tenant may raise reasons for requesting a review of the decision of the review committee, but only once. The decision of the review is compulsory and both parties should obey it. Correspondingly, we hereby send you a letter, hoping that you will check and review it. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Government."

Twenty-Six Organizations Petitioned the Judicial Yuan for Special Amnesty for Liu Chongwu and Others

To be mailed to Beijing today

The Shanghai All Circles Aid Patriotic Martyrs Committee, the Shanghai General Labor Union, the Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association of Seven Counties of Shaoxing, the Nantong Fellow Villagers Association, the National Products Manufacturers Federation, the Citizens Federation of the First Special District, the Twelfth, Seventeenth, Eighteenth, Nineteenth, Twentieth, Twenty-second, Seventeenth, Twenty-eighth, Twenty-ninth, Thirtieth, Thirty-third, Thirty-fourth, District Branches, Transportation Brick and Tile Occupational Union, South Goods Industry, Occupational Union, and other twenty-six organizations, in order to appeal for special amnesty for patriotic martyrs Liu Chongwu, Pan Hongsheng, Tian Shuiyang, Cao Songshou, etc., jointly signed and sealed (the seals were completely affixed yesterday) a petition to the Judicial Yuan (to be sent by registered mail from the post office today). The original text is as follows: "Petition for patriotic martyrs Liu Chongwu, Pan Hongsheng, Tian Shuiyang, Cao Songshou, etc., to be retried by the Supreme Court and still sentenced to severe punishment, causing public outrage. We beseech you to grant a special amnesty based on the original situation, in order to maintain the national spirit and comfort the people's hopes. Since Japan occupied the Northeast, poisoned Shanghai, and encroached upon China, its momentum has been unstoppable. The people of our country have endured this for a long time, because they are in pain from the impending doom of national subjugation and want to save the sinking situation. Soldiers vowed to fight hand-to-hand, merchants vowed to sever relations, and all matters that are beneficial to the country and resist the enemy rose up at the same time. Resistance to violence is the common desire of all people, and safeguarding the country is our unshirkable responsibility. In such circumstances, we would not hesitate to go through fire and water and would not allow for careful consideration and deliberation, as would be the case in peacetime when the advantages and disadvantages can be weighed in advance. In the winter of the twenty-first year, patriotic martyrs Liu Chongwu, Pan Hongsheng, Tian Shuiyang, Cao Songshou, etc., were angry at the enemy-collaborating merchants and the dumping of enemy goods, which led to the decline of national goods and the despair of the people's livelihood. Rather than sitting and waiting for death, why not rise up and seek survival? However, there are many obstacles, and it is often difficult to achieve results. Therefore, even legitimate work can only be carried out in secret. The cause of the Liu case was entirely to be patriotic and protect national goods. However, the enemy-collaborating merchants were blinded by profit and actively bundled and sold enemy goods, so that national goods had no place to stand. They refused to be persuaded and were forced to use dangerous goods as a final warning. Unexpectedly, a fire broke out at one time, and a catastrophe flew in, resulting in being imprisoned and suffering injustice until now. This case was first filed by Kan Jingxian, a lawyer representing the Criminal Section of the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department Police Department, to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court. The first instance verdict was that Liu Chongwu was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment, Pan Hongsheng and Cao Songshou were each sentenced to three months of imprisonment with a three-year reprieve, and Tian Shuiyang was sentenced to two months of imprisonment with a three-year reprieve. Lawyer Kan was still not satisfied and appealed again for the crime of premeditated murder. In July of last year, the second instance verdict by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court overturned the original verdict. Liu, Pan, and Cao were all sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment for conspiring to commit murder together. Tian Shuiyang was sentenced to six years of imprisonment for assisting in murder. At that time, people from all walks of life believed that the trial was inappropriate and convened an aid committee for patriotic martyrs, resolving that various groups should submit petitions to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and the Judicial Yuan for relief, and hired four lawyers, Ma Junteng, Zhang Shizhao, Yu Hualong, and Li Shirui, to appeal to the Supreme Court in order to show justice in each case. In July of this year, the Supreme Court ordered a retrial. The judgment of the retrial was that Liu Chongwu was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment, Tian Shuiyang and Pan Hongsheng were sentenced to six years of imprisonment, and Cao Songshou was still sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment. People from all walks of life believed that the sentence was still too heavy. The aid committee for patriotic martyrs convened an emergency meeting on the day of the incident and resolved that in addition to having the original lawyers file an appeal to the Judicial Yuan again, various groups should jointly sign a petition to continue to request relief. We find that the actions of Liu and others are indeed not allowed by law, but the purpose of Liu and others is indeed approved by the people of the whole country. In short, the loyalty of Liu and others to the country is obvious. It is neither a private feud nor a premeditated killing. The conscience of the people is still there, and justice still exists. We will never allow these patriotic martyrs to be imprisoned for a long time. If those who harm the country are still granted leniency, but those who love the country are punished with severe crimes, the gains and losses will be reversed, causing public outrage. The power to reverse the injustice lies with the superiors. In addition to hiring the original lawyers to petition your court to correct the situation according to the law, we hereby submit the facts again, begging your court to approve a special amnesty. The country will be fortunate, and the nation will be fortunate."

The Joint Federation of Machine Industry Associations Requests Increased Import Tax on Molasses

The Joint Federation of Machine-Made National Goods Factories of this city yesterday submitted a report to the Ministry of Finance and the National Tariff Commission, stating that they were submitting a report based on the actual situation, requesting an increase in the import tax on molasses raw materials to help rescue rural areas and maintain domestic goods. The report quoted a letter from the Meilong Perfume and Pharmaceutical Factory, a member of the federation, stating, "Our factory was established in the twelfth year of the Republic of China and specializes in the production of chemical drugs such as alcohol and menthol. It has been more than a decade since then, and we believe that we have achieved considerable results in the industry. However, since the Shanghai War, foreign goods, especially alcohol, have been continuously imported and dumped in large quantities. Taking Shanghai port as an example, the annual leakage amounts to more than 800,000 national currency, which is truly alarming. Alcohol is a necessity for the chemical industry and national defense. Our factory believes that only by expanding production can we resist foreign imports. Therefore, last year, we increased our capital and built a new factory at 802 Huishan Road, producing in large quantities to meet the needs of society. The raw materials for alcohol are extracted from agricultural products such as millet, corn, sorghum, yams, and wheat bran. Although the cost is high, at this time of rural collapse, if we can use domestic raw materials as much as possible to prevent goods from being discarded on the ground, the aid to rural areas will not be insignificant. In addition, foreign molasses is also a raw material for the production of alcohol. Foreign merchants, in order to break our country's agricultural production, deliberately lowered prices. In addition, the import tax rate on molasses is very low, only collecting 3.7 cents of Customs Gold per picul. In all countries of the world, the import tax rate is temporarily light if the raw materials are not available in the country and are necessary. However, when the country already has the same raw materials, the foreign import tax is immediately increased. This not only enriches the national tax revenue but also balances and adjusts to protect domestic raw materials from defeat. If we do not pay attention to this and allow foreign molasses to flood our country's markets, not only will industry be affected, but also the government's intention to promote the use of domestic raw materials will become a bubble. We have always admired your association's efforts to promote domestic goods. We earnestly request that you forward this report to the Ministry of Finance and the National Tariff Commission, requesting them to approve an increase in the import tax rate on foreign molasses to more than three yuan of Customs Gold per picul to show restrictions. This will be in line with the true meaning of rescuing rural areas and promoting completely domestic goods, which is a public feeling." The report also stated that the bankruptcy of rural areas is due to the discarding of goods and the decline of domestic goods is due to the reliance on foreign raw materials. Therefore, if we do not pay attention to the promotion of agricultural products and the application of domestic raw materials, and want to rescue rural areas and promote domestic goods, it is truly abandoning the root and pursuing the branches, and will ultimately be of no help. The situation reported by the Meilong Perfume and Pharmaceutical Factory is of fundamental importance. It is appropriate to prepare a document and submit it, hoping that your association will review and approve the increase in the import tariff on molasses so that both domestic goods and rural areas will benefit. Respectfully submitted.

In the afternoon of the day before yesterday, Hubei fellow-provincials in Shanghai, including Tang Xiangming, Hu Zongduo, Zhang Zhiben, Liu Wenhui, Wu Xingya, Guan Jinzhi, Wang Shaocheng, and others, held a public banquet at the Gongdelin Restaurant for people from all walks of life in Shanghai due to the severe drought and flood situation in their home province. The rest, including Jie Wenliu, Yuan Ludeng, Zhang Zhiben, Guan Jinzhi, Hu Zongduo, and Wang Shaocheng, all gave extremely heartbreaking and painful speeches. The length is not recorded. The guests and hosts dispersed happily at 8 o'clock.

River Dredging in the County Has Been Surveyed

Shanghai County's general mobilization for river dredging this year has been approved by the provincial government after the county government investigated the rivers to be dredged in each district. The Navigation Administration Bureau Issues a Circular to All Shipping Companies to Crack Down on Crew Members Who Have Not Obtained Certificates

The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications issued a circular to all Chinese shipping companies yesterday, saying:

"For your compliance, the instructions in the Ministry of Communications' No. 16847 Order state, 'Regarding Chinese and foreign crew members serving on Chinese ships who have not yet obtained certificates, they should be cracked down on by the end of this year. You should start registering unemployed crew members who have already obtained certificates for supplementary purposes. This is the order,' etc. Upon receipt of this order, it has been found that cracking down on Chinese and foreign crew members serving on Chinese ships who have not obtained corresponding certificates has been delayed due to the complicated procedures for applying for certificates and the inability to complete the examination on schedule. The ministry has repeatedly issued orders to extend the crackdown period to show consideration for all parties. Now, the extended deadline is approaching again in a blink of an eye. In order to maintain the safety of ships, this bureau will strictly comply with the ministry's order and carry out the crackdown after the deadline. It has also started registering unemployed crew members who have already obtained certificates for supplementary purposes, which was the reason for the order. In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is hereby issued for your company's reference. Within the deadline, all crew members who have not obtained corresponding certificates should be replaced to avoid this bureau issuing a deadline to replace them at that time, which may delay the sailing schedule and cause losses. Please note this order."

Injured Worker Fu Xinzhao Died in the Hospital Yesterday

The Workers' Side Has Filed a Criminal Lawsuit with the Court

According to the Ta Kung Pao, after the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory on Xujiahui Road resumed work in compliance with the order, it announced the dismissal of 103 male and female workers that evening, causing panic among the workers. Police Pick Up a Child

Sun Chungui Comes to the Station to Claim It

Shi Qingru, a watchman at No. 36 Dongmen Road, Nanshi, found a baby boy who was only one month old on the side of the road at 6:00 p.m. the other day. He found that the baby was wearing a cotton-padded jacket made of floral flannel and a skirt. He waited for a long time but no one came to claim it, which made him suspicious. He immediately took the baby back to the station and asked for instructions. Director Liu suspected that the baby was an abandoned illegitimate child or that there was another reason. He was about to send the baby to the church for foster care when Sun Chungui, a Tongzhou native who lived in Pudong Lan Ni Du and worked at the British-American Tobacco Factory, came to the station and claimed that the baby was his son, who was only a month old. He said that his wife, Sun Tao, had come to visit him with the baby, but had hired a car to the ferry terminal at Dadongmen. She had suddenly fainted and dropped the baby on the ground without realizing it. She did not know until she returned home in Pudong and her aunt saw her come back empty-handed and asked about the baby. She could not answer and fell asleep in a daze. Now that she has recovered a little, she has realized what happened and asked to claim the baby. Director Liu checked the statement and found that the baby could not speak and could not prove it. He asked Sun Chungui to provide a reliable shop guarantee and wait for verification before claiming the baby.

Completion of the Largest Police Station in the Far East

The Completion Ceremony Will Be Held on New Year's Day

Ten Stories High and Equipped with a Wireless Radio Station

The new Central Police Station of the Public Works Department, the largest in scale in the Far East, has now been completed. It is currently being decorated internally, and a completion ceremony is planned for New Year's Day next year. The authorities will also invite consuls from various countries and leaders from all walks of life to visit. The China Eastern News Agency reporter has made a special visit and recorded the following:

Construction Process: The Central Police Station of the Public Works Department on Fuzhou Road, west of the department, has been built for many years and is no longer suitable for use. The police station is only four stories high, which is not enough for office space. Therefore, the department decided to build a new one across from the department, east of the YMCA and west of the Bank of Communications, through a board resolution last year. Bidding was invited in the summer of last year, and after more than a year, it was completely completed the other day.

Internal Allocation: The new police station building is about 100 feet high, covers an area of three mu, and has a total of ten stories. According to the spokesman of the department, the first floor of the new building is the interrogation section and the vehicle office; the second floor is the office of the Chinese superintendent, the Indian deputy superintendent, and the Chinese deputy superintendent; the third floor is the showroom and the photography room; the fourth floor is the police salary room, the anti-drug room, the investigation section, the private handgun license room, and the chief inspector of Chinese detectives; the fifth floor is the office of the police commissioner, the deputy police commissioner, and the confidential document storage room; the sixth floor is the fingerprint section and the criminal case file room; the seventh floor is the political affairs department and the film censorship section; the eighth and ninth floors are the clubhouse, with a billiard room, a coffee shop, a wine bar, and a library; and the tenth floor is the office of the wireless radio station and the telephone room and the typing room. There are also two wireless radio poles on the roof, which can communicate with the patrol cars at any time, and a part of it is used as a dormitory.

Largest in the Far East: The new building is named the Central Police Station. All of the current Central Police Station will be moved to the new building for office work. After the completion of the new building, it will not only be the leading police agency in Shanghai, but even the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department in Japan is not as good. It can be said to be the largest police station in the Far East. The construction cost is one million yuan. The department will wait for the internal decoration to be completely completed and plans to hold a completion ceremony on New Year's Day next year, inviting consuls from various countries and Chinese and Western leaders to visit.

A Small Steamer Overturns a Rowboat

The Body of Yang Asan Was Retrieved and Examined

Yang Asan, a native of Zhapu, Zhejiang, was 41 years old. He had been running a bamboo weaving shop in the Hujunying area of Nanshi, specializing in making yellow baskets for loading coal balls in coal ball factories. On the morning of the 16th of this month, at 11:00 a.m., Yang Asan and his son Yang Ada hired a rowboat at the Xuejiabang Wharf to load 1,000 yellow baskets, each priced at six cents, for a total value of sixty yuan, and transported them to the Yuanhe Coal Ball Factory, which had newly opened in the Lan Ni Du Town of Pudong, for delivery. When the rowboat sailed to the outer wharf of the Da Matou, the Xin Ren Chang small steamer, also heading north from the south, was advancing by paddling. Due to careless driving, it slammed into the rowboat. Because the force was too great, the rowboat was immediately overturned, and both people and goods fell into the water. Yang Ada and the boatman were rescued and survived, but Yang Asan's body disappeared and was taken by the god of the sea. At that time, the water patrol team arrested Zhang Xinkang and Xu Cuilin, the drivers who caused the accident, and handed them over to the team for transfer to the local court for interrogation and imprisonment. Yang Asan's body was retrieved by the rescue bureau's patrol boat in the Pu yesterday morning and taken to the Pu beach at the South Wharf. Yang Ada, the son of the deceased, and Yang Tang, the wife of the deceased, went to identify the body and confirmed that it was correct. They then filed a request with the local court for an examination. After receiving the report, the court immediately commissioned Prosecutor Ouyang Shu and other examiners, including Xuan Zhiming, to go to the scene for examination and instructed the family to put the body in a coffin and wait for further investigation.

A Woman Drowns in the Clear Stream

She Takes Off Her Qipao and Throws Herself into the Pu River

At about 11:00 p.m. the other night, a woman of about 20 years old suddenly ran alone to the outer embankment of the Jinliyuan No. 7 Wharf on the Bund, took off a lined qipao made of blue woolen fabric with a red plaid lining, and immediately jumped into the Pu River to commit suicide. The nearby boatmen caught a glimpse of her and rushed to rescue her, but it was too late. The woman was submerged in the muddy current in an instant, and her body sank and disappeared. The Chinese police from the Xiaodongmen police station arrived and took the qipao back to the French police station and telegraphed the customs water patrol police station to investigate. The woman took off her long clothes before committing suicide, seemingly hoping to sink more easily after entering the water, which shows her determination to take this last road.

The Detective Office Formally Indicts Lu Xihou and Others

Disclosing the True Story of the Collapse of the China Xingye Bank

Currently Being Prosecuted for Fraud, Additional Charges May Be Filed

丨 Both Defendants' Requests for Bail Were Rejected 丨

After Qin Baoyuan, the manager of China Xingye Bank, absconded with a large sum of money, the bank immediately collapsed on October 11th, declaring liquidation. All promissory notes that matured were not honored. Mitsui & Co., a Japanese firm in this city, sold artificial silk worth 6,405 yuan to Dashengchang Grocery Store last month. The store issued a China Xingye Bank promissory note for 7,690 yuan, payable on the first of this month. At the time, Mitsui refunded 16 yuan in cash and 1,654 yuan in local currency notes. However, when the note matured, Xingye Bank was unable to redeem it. Mitsui then filed a complaint with the General Detective Office. After investigation by Chinese detectives Zhang Mingde, Kang Zengxiang, and Liu Xiangzhai, they obtained an arrest warrant from the First Special Court. The chairman of the China Xingye Bank board of directors, Lu Xihou, a local (resident at 51 Longmen Road), and Sun Xiren, the manager of Dashengchang Grocery Store, from Hangzhou (resident at 551 Datong Road), were arrested at 3 PM the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to Division One of the First Special Court, where Judge Qian Hongye presided over the hearing. The detective office was represented by lawyer Ru Baoyi, while Lu and Sun were defended by lawyers Wu Linkun, Fan Gang, Zhang Ding, and others. The detective office's lawyer then presented the

Intention to Prosecute and Legal Articles, stating that the prosecution was being brought under Articles 363 and 366 of the Criminal Code for the crimes of fraud and breach of trust. Lu Xihou was also suspected of violating the Banking Law and Savings Law, but due to the complexity of the case, this has not yet been determined, and prosecution will occur later. It was found that in 1932, when China Xingye Bank could not be maintained, Lu Xihou and two others organized the Qunyi Banking Syndicate, investing a total of 225,000 yuan to acquire the bank. However, two of the investors soon withdrew, leaving Lu as the sole proprietor. The bank was neither legally organized nor registered with the Ministry of Finance, so its internal affairs were extremely corrupt. In addition to conducting ordinary banking business, the bank also engaged in savings, offering particularly high interest rates, thus attracting a large amount of deposits from ordinary people. Lu also ran the Huili Ball Court, Xiaoshijie Amusement Park, and Guomin Hotel, and recently organized an international horse racing club, which was

A Disguised Form of Gambling. Because a license could not be obtained, it has been delayed for over three months. The club has purchased 150 horses, each costing 1,000 yuan, requiring 150,000 yuan. Jockeys, etc., were hired from abroad, so daily expenses amounted to 1,000 taels of silver. Therefore, the deposits absorbed by Xingye Bank were transferred for use in the horse racing club. Still fearing insufficiency, the Xinhua Trading Company and Dashengchang Grocery Store, founded by Qin Baoyuan as subsidiaries of Xingye Bank, purchased large quantities of goods from various merchants, paying for them with Xingye Bank promissory notes that could not be cashed. The goods were then sold cheaply the next day to obtain cash to maintain the horse racing club. The defendant, Sun Xiren, helped make this plan successful. It was found that Qin Baoyuan, the manager of Xingye Bank, absconded on the 24th of last month. Lu initially did not announce this. It was not until October 1st, when Mitsui's promissory notes were about to mature, that he reported to the detective office, claiming that the manager had

Embezzled a Huge Sum and Fled. His intention was that this pretense would give him a plausible excuse for not paying the promissory notes and declaring liquidation. Unexpectedly, Mitsui was not fooled. They reported it to the detective office. After investigation by the detective office, the above situation was fully discovered. Furthermore, after the bank collapsed, when the detective office staff maintained order at the bank's entrance, the sight of ordinary poor depositors gathering at the bank gate to hear news was particularly distressing. It was found that the names listed as directors and supervisors of the bank were all fictitious, with only Lu in charge. Therefore, it was requested that the court issue an arrest warrant. However, the circumstances of the case were complex, and a request was made to postpone the hearing. At that time, the detective office may file additional charges, etc. Then, Arjuna, a representative of Mitsui & Co., described the transaction and receipt of the promissory notes. Judge Qian stated that the case was complex and ordered a special hearing to be scheduled for this Friday afternoon. The defendants' lawyers requested bail, but this was rejected.

Lasting Two Hours

Inquiries Were Extremely Detailed

Trial Continues Today

Yu Baosan and Son Nearly Kidnapped

Fortunately, the Car Had a Secret Braking Mechanism

The Bandits Were Unable to Drive the Car and Abandoned the Hostages and Fled

Yu Baosan, a native of Ningbo, 54 years old, lives at No. 176 Weihaiwei Road. He has eight sons. His fourth son, Shuangqing, works at the Tongyuan Bank at No. 50 Tianjin Road. Yu himself runs the Chenxingji Real Estate Department at No. 349 Ningbo Road. Therefore, Mr. Yu and his son always drive their own sedan car to work every morning. The driver is Xu Yuquan, a native of Shaoxing. Yesterday morning at 8:40, Mr. Yu and his son walked out of their home as usual and got into their car. At that time, Wang Guoqing, the doorman of Jinle Lane, from Shandong, saw this and immediately stepped forward to close the car door. The driver, Xu Yuquan, also turned the engine switch, preparing to drive off. Unexpectedly, at that moment, suddenly five or six bandits, one wearing a long robe and the others wearing short clothes, jumped out from the roadside, pushed the doorman into the lane entrance, and two bandits jumped into the car compartment where Mr. Yu and his son were sitting, watching them with guns. Two bandits jumped into the front of the car and dragged the driver out of the car and drove off themselves. The driver and the doorman were shocked and screamed for help. They turned around and saw a Westerner's car parked nearby at the entrance of Xianglin Lane. Fearing that the bandits would escape, the doorman and the driver ran to the Westerner for help. At this time, the bandit driving the car was turning the engine switch, hoping to drive away, but unexpectedly, the car was equipped with a secret braking mechanism, which had already been locked by Mr. Yu and his son, so the bandits were unable to start the car. Seeing that the situation was not good, they abandoned the hostages, got out of the car, and fled in different directions to the east. Wang Guoqing, the doorman, saw this and immediately followed closely behind one of the bandits, hoping to take the opportunity to arrest him. When they reached No. 174 Weihaiwei Road, he saw the bandit throw what he was holding into the house and run away empty-handed. Wang Guoqing saw an opportunity and was about to arrest him when suddenly a bandit jumped out from behind him, pointed a gun at Wang Guoqing, and ordered him to retreat. Wang had no choice but to stand by the side of the road, allowing the bandits to escape. At that time, detectives from the Chengdu Road Detective Office also received a report and rushed to the scene, but the bandits had already fled far away and could not be arrested. They went to No. 174 to investigate and found a four-inch pistol discarded by the bandits, containing seven bullets, as well as a blue cloth short shirt and a broken shoe. Looking back at Mr. Yu and his son, their faces were pale and they were still terrified. They were immediately sent back to their residence. The fingerprints in the car were carefully examined and taken back to the detective office for investigation, so as to track down the criminals.

Englishman Killed in Car Accident, Chinese Man Injured and Charged

Englishman Dies from Reckless Driving

Chinese Man Injured in Car Accident Acquitted

Du Decheng, a native of Yangzhou and the chief cashier of the Wuxi Zhongnan Bank, came to Shanghai for business during the Double Tenth Festival and resided at the Kaitai Hotel on Tianjin Road. At 12:40 PM on the 14th of this month, Du was walking across the road at Jing'an Temple Road and Carter Road when Douglas, a British accountant from the British-American Tramway Company, passed by on a motorized bicycle. Because of his skillful driving and excessive speed, he was unable to avoid a collision. As a result, Du Decheng suffered injuries to his head and legs, and the Englishman fell from the bicycle, injuring his brain, and died without receiving medical treatment. When the detective office learned of this, they brought Du Decheng into the detective office for being careless while walking. The next morning, he was escorted to the First Special Court, where it was ordered that Du be released on 500 yuan bail. News of this was reported. It is now reported that Judge Wu Yanqi continued to hear the case in the Eighth Criminal Court yesterday morning. The defendant hired lawyer E Sen to defend him, while the detective office determined that Du Decheng was negligent in walking and prosecuted him for causing death by negligence under Article 291 of the Criminal Code. The detective office's lawyer Zhang Tianyin then presented the case, and officer No. 325 testified that the defendant did not pay attention to the passing vehicles when crossing the road, causing the accident. Witness Gu Jiannong testified that he was an employee of the Shanghai Bank branch at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Tongfu Road. On the day of the accident, it was Sunday, and he finished work at 12:00. Because a tailor was coming to make a suit, he was chatting with his colleague Qian Tianyou in a room on the third floor. Before long, he suddenly heard a strange sound of a car stopping on the road downstairs. He looked out the window and saw a motorized bicycle overturned to the north, and an Englishman lying down. A Chinese man was lying on the ground to the south. I did not see the collision, but according to my guess, the motorcycle must have been going too fast and had passed the car in front of it, causing it to brake suddenly and make a strange sound. The person also fell from the bicycle, etc. Qian Tianyou also testified that he was looking out of the window on the third floor of the Shanghai Bank when he suddenly saw the defendant walking to the middle of the road. The deceased suddenly crashed into him from the right at great speed. There is no doubt that the deceased was driving too fast. Du Decheng was questioned and stated that there were no vehicles when he crossed the road. When he reached the middle of the road, the deceased's car suddenly crashed into him, injuring his head and legs, and he has not yet recovered and has difficulty walking. Lawyer E Sen then argued that the deceased had only been in Shanghai from England for three months and had no driving experience. Moreover, on that day, he was driving too fast, which caused the brakes to be affected. The person fell from the bicycle and landed on the ground, six feet away from the car, which shows that his speed was too high and it was not easy to stop suddenly. However, it was found that the accident site was at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Carter Road, where vehicles were constantly passing by. The deceased should not have been traveling at such a high speed, which caused the accident. Therefore, the deceased was at fault, and the defendant was not involved. Moreover, the defendant is now seriously injured and should be acquitted. Judge Wu reviewed the testimony and acquitted Du Decheng in court.

Declaration of the Shanghai Women's Progressive Association

The modern era has encountered a major transformation of social values in various aspects. In the process of building a new culture caused by the inevitable conclusion of modern civilization, the liberation of women, who have been neglected for thousands of years but occupy a very important position in human evolution, has become one of the important tasks of the present day. Regarding this point, only those who calmly observe the trends of the times and the path of modern civilization will not overlook this fact. Originally, the so-called women's movement carries two meanings. On the passive side, it is the general awareness of women who seek to break away from the problem of male dependence and subordination. On the active side, in addition to the liberation of women themselves, it is a fundamental issue related to the progress of the entire nation. In other words, the task of the women's movement must include not only seeking the liberation and improvement of women's own status and the cultivation of virtues, but also engaging in social production and promoting its ability to the nation-state. Therefore, this issue is not only a problem for women themselves, but also a link in the evolutionary development process of the country and nation. Historical records indicate that the nineteenth century was truly an era in which the destruction of the old lives of women, who had been groaning in cruel bondage for thousands of years, and the creation of a new, vibrant life for women were advancing side by side. At that time, because all countries were in the process of this destruction and construction, the women's movement throughout the world made great progress. Therefore, although our country, which received the opportunity to accept this new trend of thought later due to various objective environments, has had several decades of history in the women's movement, we, though not completely blindly negating the achievements made, can at least only critically accept its results at this moment. Especially in the work of the past few years, generally speaking, only the slogan of women's participation in politics has been shouted out, and some passive relief work has been done, while neglecting its main aspect. It is an undeniable and well-known fact that it has not helped women's future and social welfare. However, on the other hand, there are currently some people in society attempting to revive this erroneous path, which further shows that women themselves have reached an even more dangerous stage today. This danger, under the protection of a clever trick, transfers the fate of women's future from the old bondage to a new bondage. This should be that the development stage of the women's movement itself has encountered a very serious crisis again. Here, we should rise up to break through this historical repetition. However, we are unwilling to sing high-sounding tunes that are too far from reality, so we will not reveal any great and eternal plans here. We only want to do some practical things in this movement, that is, we only want to provide all our intelligence to improve and obtain the general status and equal opportunities for women in society, and indirectly serve the country, nation, and society. Needless to say, in the evolution and development of all living things, sexual differentiation and sexual opposition occupy a very important position. However, there is definitely no meaning of domination, subordination, and determining superiority and inferiority in this. This has already been the conclusion obtained by various parties in the modern era. Therefore, we must enable all our women to obtain complete freedom and complete independence in all aspects. However, in order to achieve the complete realization of this task, the economic subordination of women to men must be eliminated, and the shackles imposed on women by the general society must be broken. This point should always be placed at the forefront of the women's movement agenda. Because until today, women in general have not been able to remove all their own special living conditions, and these conditions are still concentrated in their special status. Therefore, the program to be performed in our future movement is to focus on how to enable women in general to eliminate their economic subordination to men, that is, special living conditions, and how to break the heavy shackles imposed on women by society, that is, inhuman living conditions. In other words, to provide women in general with the necessary weapons, that is, intelligence, to eliminate this economic subordination to men and the heavy shackles bestowed by society, so as to cultivate completely free and independent people, so as to prepare to be social warriors, and to accomplish their social service as new virtuous wives and good mothers. In addition, we also deeply realize that the women's movement will not succeed in a society under the feudal system, and at the same time, the women's movement will not be allowed to succeed in a society under the capitalist system. Therefore, we have come to this understanding that only under the social system of the Three Principles of the People can the women's movement develop to a higher stage and complete its entire task. We hold this enthusiastic wish, which is not very, and with the spirit of sacrifice and service, we engage in the practice of focusing on the big picture and starting with the small things, and with a very sincere attitude, we hope that all women in society will participate, work hard, and be active. At the same time, we stand on the perspective of the entire nation and eagerly hope that gentlemen with a group consciousness will give us assistance, guidance, and criticism. This is our declaration.

Single-Direction Traffic Plan Moved to Jiujiang Road, Taxpayers Association Asks for Cancellation of Proposal

The Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association yesterday sent a letter to the Secretary of the Public Works Department, stating: "Sir, we have received a letter from the Eighteenth District Branch of the Shanghai Special District No. 1 Citizens' Federation, which states: 'Having read in the newspapers that various businesses on Hankou Road have requested the cancellation of the one-way traffic plan on that road, the Public Works Department has transferred the request to the Traffic Committee for consideration and submission to the Board of Directors for approval. After discussion, the committee concluded that the one-way traffic on Hankou Road is more beneficial than harmful and decided to temporarily shelve the protests of the businesses on that road, pending reports from the police and public works departments on whether one-way traffic can be implemented on Jiujiang Road. We understand that the businesses on Hankou Road want to cancel the one-way traffic because it affects their business. Now, the Public Works Department intends to implement the one-way traffic that Hankou Road merchants do not want on Jiujiang Road. Moreover, Jiujiang Road is narrower than Hankou Road, and there are more shops, many of which are small businesses. If one-way traffic is implemented, the business of the shops on Jiujiang Road will be unimaginable. Our federation cannot remain silent on this harmful and useless road policy of the Public Works Department. We are writing to request that you forward this letter to the Public Works Department, asking them to cancel the one-way traffic plan on Jiujiang Road to ease the difficulties of the businesses. We would be most grateful.'" The letter was received by the association and we are accordingly writing to request that your bureau comply with public opinion and cancel the proposal, in order to maintain the business of the shops on that road. This is addressed to the Secretary of the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department.

Two Organizations Defend Dr. Zhong Juemin Against False Accusations

The Shanghai Physicians Association sent a letter to the Municipal Police Bureau on behalf of Dr. Zhong Juemin, who has been falsely accused, requesting a public clarification. The letter stated: "Sir, we have received a letter from Mr. Zhong Zhimin, the brother of our member Zhong Juemin, which states: 'My brother Juemin has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for seventeen years, has been law-abiding, and has never engaged in improper behavior. However, a man named Zhong Minggeng was arrested by your bureau's detective team on Fangbang Road in Ximen for selling red pills. He falsely claimed that Juemin was his relative and that the red pills were bought by Juemin's servant. On August 25th, officers from your bureau's detective team escorted Zhong Minggeng to the Xinzha police station in the Public Concession to request an investigation. The Xinzha police station summoned Juemin and his cook Zhao Donglin for questioning. Fortunately, it was found that Zhong Minggeng did not know Zhong Juemin or Zhao Donglin at all, and his statements were completely false. It was also discovered that Juemin was a legitimate doctor of many years. They were told to go home and resume their business. However, on the 16th of this month, the Shanghai Special District No. 1 District Court issued an arrest warrant, and Juemin and Zhao Donglin were arrested and detained. We are writing this letter to request assistance.'" After investigation, Dr. Zhong Juemin is indeed a member of our association, and his scholarship and ethics are well known to our colleagues. It seems unjust that he is being unfairly suppressed based solely on Zhong Minggeng's one-sided false accusations, which are completely unsubstantiated. This makes law-abiding residents feel endangered and fearful. After discussion at the Sixth Regular Meeting of our Eighth Executive Committee, we decided to send a letter to your bureau requesting a clarification. We are accordingly writing to request that you investigate and handle this matter. We would be most grateful. This is addressed to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, from the Shanghai Physicians Association."

Also, the Shaoxing Seven Counties Shanghai Compatriots Association sent a letter to the Police Bureau, stating: "Sir, our fellow townsman Zhong Juemin has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for seventeen years, with excellent skills and social recognition. However, a man named Zhong Minggeng was arrested by the Shanghai Municipal Detective Team for selling red pills. He falsely claimed that Zhong Juemin was a relative and that the red pills were bought from Zhong Juemin's servant. On August 25th, officers from the Municipal Police Bureau's Detective Team escorted Zhong Minggeng to the Xinzha police station in the Public Concession to request an investigation. After questioning by the police station, it was determined that Zhong Minggeng did not know Zhong Juemin or his cook Zhao Donglin at all, and his statements were false. They were told to go home and resume their business. However, on the 16th of this month, the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau requested the Shanghai Special District No. 1 District Court to issue an arrest warrant. Together with Chinese and foreign detectives from the Xinzha police station, they went to Zhong Juemin's clinic and arrested Zhong Juemin and Zhao Donglin. On the morning of the 17th, they were sent to the No. 1 Special District Court for trial. The police station stated that there was no conclusive evidence against Zhong Juemin and Zhao Donglin and that they had not committed any crimes. They requested a detailed investigation and a postponement of the interrogation. Although the court approved a seven-day postponement and ordered the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau to bring Zhong Minggeng for questioning next time, Zhong Juemin and Zhao Donglin are already being detained at the police station. Zhong Juemin is a law-abiding doctor. This time, he was falsely accused and detained by Zhong Minggeng, whom he does not know, along with his cook Zhao Donglin. This is extremely unjust. In addition to sending a separate letter to the No. 1 Special District Court, we respectfully request that you strictly investigate Zhong Minggeng, who is being detained in your department, in order to deter unlawful acts and reassure law-abiding citizens. We would be most grateful. This is addressed to Wu, the Songhu Garrison Commander, from Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, and Pei Yunqing, the chairmen and vice-chairmen of the Shaoxing Seven Counties Shanghai Compatriots Association."

New Medicine Association Defends Starlight Pharmaceutical Factory Against False Accusations

The New Medicine Association submitted a report to the Municipal Police Bureau yesterday, stating: "We are submitting this report because a member has been falsely accused and we request that the relevant parties be released on bail during the chemical testing period. According to a letter from our affiliated member, Wanguo Pharmacy, the products manufactured by its affiliated Starlight Pharmaceutical Factory have been tested by pharmacists and found to be free of prohibited drugs. On the morning of the 21st of this month, the Second Branch of the Police Bureau suddenly seized compound calomel pills, arsenous acid pills, red tonic pills, appetite-stimulating sugar, compound laxative pills, and other drugs, and detained ten employees. We request that you forward a letter to the bureau requesting their release." We immediately sent a letter and asked Sun Choucheng, the person in charge of the association, to visit Director Li of the branch bureau to explain everything. Director Li said that the case was reported by Ma Wujiu, Sang Jinhai, and Long Bingyan, who claimed that the factory was privately manufacturing red pills, so they immediately went to search the factory. However, since there were no raw materials for manufacturing red pills, they only took various drugs to the bureau for testing. They have already interrogated the reporters and four key personnel from the factory, including Wen Yutang, and sent them to the main bureau. The remaining six people can be released on bail, and Da Kang Pharmacy has already posted bail for them. The drugs manufactured by the pharmaceutical factory are all produced and managed under the supervision of licensed pharmacists. The drugs seized this time cannot be substituted for red pills and can be sent to the Health Bureau for testing. However, during the testing period, we request that your bureau handle this matter in accordance with Article 2 of the improved drug inspection measures jointly formulated with the Health Bureau in the past, and temporarily release the suspects on appropriate bail to avoid harming innocent people. If the testing results confirm that the drugs can be substituted for red pills, the guarantor will be responsible for handing over the guaranteed parties. Otherwise, the three reporters should be prosecuted for false accusations."

U.S. Consular Court Investigates Sailor Assault Case

The *Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury* reported that the SS President Jefferson of the Dollar Steamship Lines, recently departed from the United States bound for Manila, when it stopped in Yokohama on October 12th. Two sailors on board were assaulted by eight sailors from the engine room, sustaining serious injuries. The captain of the ship sent a wireless telegraph to Shanghai during the voyage. Therefore, when the ship arrived in Shanghai, an officer from the U.S. Consular Court, assisted by the water police, boarded the ship and arrested the eight sailors. The cases of two of the sailors were more serious, and they were released on bail of US$1,000 each. The remaining six sailors were each released on bail of $100. The case was heard by U.S. Consular Judge Hillermeier this morning (22nd) at 10:00 AM. The plaintiff was first questioned about the circumstances of the assault. After the questioning, the defendant's lawyer, Davis, argued that according to the plaintiff's testimony, the ship was docked at the Yokohama wharf when the assault occurred. Therefore, the U.S. Consular Court in China had no jurisdiction over the case and it should be tried by the Yokohama Japanese court. After the statement, the U.S. Consular Judge stated that there was a significant question as to whether the court should accept the case. District Attorney Huaxiannai requested an adjournment until 2:00 PM to continue the hearing so that he could thoroughly study this point. The U.S. Consular Judge agreed and adjourned the court.

Datong Bookstore Holds Arithmetic Game

The Datong Bookstore on Fourth Malu, Shanghai, has been holding an arithmetic game since October 20th. The game consists of ten arithmetic problems with the addition, subtraction, multiplication, and division signs and answers missing. Participants are asked to fill in the blanks. The original answers have been prepared and sealed in advance and displayed in the store's window. Anyone who purchases Chinese and foreign books and stationery, subscribes to magazines, or commissions the printing of large and small print jobs worth 50 cents or more at the bookstore will receive an arithmetic game sheet. More purchases entitle one to more sheets. The sheets are to be filled out in the prescribed manner. If the answers match or are closest to the original answers after the reveal, one can win a huge prize. The first prize is a Stewart-Warner eight-tube floor-model radio. The second prize and below include five-tube radios, organs, harmonicas, and other valuable gifts. Regardless of whether one wins a prize, all filled-out game sheets submitted to the bookstore can be exchanged for a ten-cent book coupon. The game is very interesting and the procedures are very simple. Therefore, participation has been extremely enthusiastic in recent days.

Central Bank Inspection Report

212th Time

The 212th Central Bank Issuance Preparation Inspection Report stated: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this council is responsible for inspecting the gold reserve for exchange of notes issued by the bank. Today, October 20, 23rd year of the Republic of China, the 212th inspection was conducted at the Issuance Bureau of this bank. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: A. Total amount of exchange notes issued: $82,765,960 in silver dollars, including: $76,461,804 in silver dollar notes and $6,304,156 in subsidiary currency notes. Total amount of exchange note reserve: $82,765,960, including: $66,587,960 in cash reserve in silver dollars. This cash reserve includes $62,896,492 stored in the bank's issuance vault, $1,889,043 stored in branch banks in various cities, and $1,800,242.25 deposited with peer banks. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to $16,178,000 in silver dollars. B. Total amount of customs gold unit exchange notes issued: $373,324.70. Total amount of customs gold unit exchange note reserve: $373,324.70. This reserve includes 7,351 taels, 9 mace, and 5 fen of gold, which at a fixed price of .50779 is equivalent to $373,324.70 in customs gold units. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's Exchange Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guaranteed reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guaranteed reserve is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is hereby issued. October 22, 23rd year of the Republic of China, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank; Supervisors: Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiluo."
