Grains

Flour Futures Rise Due to Short Covering

丨Pressure from Sell-offs Before Close丨

The flour market opened higher yesterday, continuing the upward momentum from the previous day's close. Market sentiment was universally bullish, and buying interest was as strong as the day before. Fuxin Mill, with a substantial number of outstanding contracts for the current month, sought to cover them at small profits, further exacerbating the urgency to cover shorts. New long positions from speculators and large outside investors were very active, with domestic and international sentiment aligned upwards. The market opened higher in the afternoon due to soaring gold prices, further boosting the upward momentum. Prices rose by four and a half to three cents compared to the previous day's closing price. Subsequently, Fuxin stopped issuing contracts, and Fufeng sold off, leveling the market. However, the closing price was still significantly higher than the previous weekend, with the current month up 2.75 cents, the next month up 2.5 cents, December up 3 cents, January up 2.25 cents, and February up 1.75 cents.

New Longs Drive Up Forward Wheat Prices

After the wheat market opened yesterday, current-month contracts saw profit-taking, with prices falling slightly by three or four cents. However, as soon as trading reached the far months, new long positions from both inside and outside the industry rushed to buy. The flour market was rising, and while foreign wheat was slightly lower, gold prices were significantly higher, attracting new long positions and short covering. In addition, the appetite of existing wheat mills was active, and prices also rose gradually. Therefore, near-month contracts also rose by five or six cents in the afternoon. In addition to short covering, far-month contracts saw aggressive buying from new long positions, leading to even greater gains. Although profit-taking later occurred, briefly leveling prices, the market ultimately rose. The closing price for the current month was up 3 cents, November and December each up 8 cents, and January up 11 cents. Current-month wheat mills took 14,000 bags, opening at a high of $3.70, with prices varying based on quality, up 10 cents from the previous weekend.

Large-Scale Activity in Native Coarse Rice Sales

丨High Prices for Foreign Rice Futures丨

The foreign native rice market was lively yesterday. Native rice prices increased, becoming increasingly popular and rapidly selling out, causing the market to rise steadily. Yesterday, native street traders aggressively competed for native coarse rice, offering 4,000 bags each of Hankou and Shashi coarse rice, causing prices to rise by five or six cents to nearly a dime. Arrivals and stockpiles of foreign native rice were low, supporting the market at a high of six or seven cents. Spot foreign rice supplies were not abundant, supporting the market. However, the new crop of pointed rice from areas downriver was entering the market, and demand was not active, leading to a firm but stagnant market situation. However, futures prices were rising, gradually increasing since the silver issue arose, leading to a gradual decline in new transactions. Yesterday, October contracts returned at $4.90, with only 100 tons traded, as囤户 (speculative merchants) were also bullish and unwilling to sell.

River Rice Market: Weak in the South, Brisk in the North

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, the arrival of rice from various sources was relatively plentiful, totaling over 30 boats, with about 4,500 to 4,600 石 (a unit of dry measure) of goods. Sales of 窰種 (kiln-dried seed rice) were limited to the local market, while foreign buyers continued to purchase. 青島幫 (Qingdao traders) took over 800 bags. However, due to the larger volume of arrivals, sentiment was slightly subdued, and the market, initially appearing tight, ended up softening by a few cents. Other varieties such as white rice, wild rice, and thick new粳 (japonica rice) saw weaker local demand, leading to a quiet market with prices falling by about 10 cents. 杜洋尖 (Du Yang pointed rice) also showed signs of weakness due to oversupply. Only various broken米(broken rice) varieties were unaffected, and demand for new陰飯担 (newly harvested and shade-dried rice) was sluggish, presenting a soft market sentiment.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 11 or 12 boats arrived with rice from various river ports, and river inventories remained low at approximately 70-80 boats. The market was active across various varieties, including new粳, broken粳, new Du pointed rice, aged white rice, and small-scale消續化 (continuously selling). New Yang pointed rice was scarce and selling slowly, while 窰種 was in active demand. New and aged 埠 (wharf rice), foreign pointed rice, and 陰元 (Yinyuan rice) were also sought after. Prices for broken粳, new粳, and aged white rice showed a slight softening trend, while 窰種 rice rose by 20-30 cents. New Du pointed rice added a few cents. New and aged 陳埠 (Chen埠 rice) and 客羊尖 (Ke Yang pointed rice) stood firm, with 元 (Yuan rice) adding 10 cents.

Black Sesame Prices Plummet Rapidly

New Yellow Soybeans Gradually Decline

Since the new Jiujiang black sesame crop entered the market just over ten days ago, prices have been falling daily from the first batch until yesterday. This is due to the large supply and limited sales, forcing sellers to lower prices to stimulate demand. Yesterday's market price was down another 40-50 cents compared to the previous Saturday. Central market goods were only offered at $6, down $2.90 from the initial price. White sesame remained stable, but high-quality goods softened slightly due to unfavorable conditions for Western traders. Yesterday's total market transaction volume for all types of sesame was over 1,000 bags, and prices continued to decline by a small margin. New yellow soybeans showed stable prices for high-quality goods, but secondary grades saw a gradual decline due to weakening demand and continued supply, leading to a sluggish market. Arrivals of new Pudong Du soybeans and Chongming new sand yellow soybeans were scarce, only 20-30 bags, so the market remained relatively stable.

Sugar Market

White Sugar Sheet Prices Rise by 50 Cents

Yesterday's sugar market should have seen prices rise in line with the increase in standard gold and customs gold, but sales did not increase as a result. Therefore, the trend remained flat and weak. The guild quoted 24 coarse granulated white ordinary spot sugar at $18.90, unchanged. Local warehouse goods were at $18.95, down 5 cents. Transshipment goods were at $5.80, down 1 cent. Dutch red sugar saw little change, with limited sales. Local factory refined white sugar was down a small dime, with higher grades at $17.60 for No. 1, $17.30 for No. 2, $17.00 for No. 3, and $16.70 for No. 4. Taikoo sugar was down a small two dimes, with B mark at $19.80, CW mark at $19.50, DY mark at $19.30, and HX mark at $19.10. There were not many transactions in graded goods, but it was heard that a certain firm sold 700 bags of white sugar sheets, with prices up 50 cents from before.

Dried Fruits: Tense Market Sentiment for Walnuts, Dates, and Dried Longans

The previous market for hand-picked walnuts had reached $24, but recently dropped by $2-3, causing tension. Yesterday at around 5 pm, news from Tianjin indicated that all grades of peaches suddenly rose by $2. Market prices today are bound to rise accordingly. According to reports, dates are also being purchased by outside traders, causing a tightening trend. The market should rise without falling. Since price drop, Tong An dried longans have seen their market settle gradually. Yesterday, due to customer requests, prices were increased by $2-3. Newly arriving goods are being held back and not sold in anticipation of rising prices. Market prices are also bound to rise accordingly, as this product is the most reasonably priced among all grades of dried longans.

Oil Market

New Crop White Tung Oil Nearing Arrival

Since a Western firm in 漠市 (Moshan) sold 100 tons of white tung oil for $28.40 per担 (picul) based on Western standards, transactions have only been in the dozens of tons in the past few days, and the market has remained unchanged. Although the Western firm is not continuing to do business, supplies are also scarce, so the situation is still stable. However, the new 台新 (Taiwanese new oil) is imminent, and the old oil market has become weak. It cannot be used as a standard, and all locations are focusing on pricing new oil. The prices being quoted in 漢市 (Hankou) a few days ago were only around $25, but there has been no further business. There is a possibility for further price drops. Zhejiang tung oil is also gradually weakening. Wenzhou oil is being offered for delivery in November at $25.50 per 砠 (bushel). Although there are no reports of similar offerings in Hangzhou, the prices are likely to be similar to Wenzhou oil. Local Western firms have also been conducting a small number of futures transactions, reportedly for November delivery at prices of $26.40-26.45 per担 (picul), supposedly conducted by Japanese firms, but the truth is unknown.

Asphalt Prices Have Fallen to the Bottom

丨Expected Strong Sales Market After New Crop Arrival丨

The new asphalt crop is nearing harvest, while inventories of old oil remain high and sales are extremely poor. Letters from Hankou detail a continuous stream of supplies and only sporadic sales. As a result, heavy 荆 (Jingzhou) oil has reached $14 after import duties, while plain 荆 oil is only at $13.30-13.40, and Macheng oil is around $13. Although local traders have little inventory, sales are nearly nonexistent. The market is listless and sentiment is depressed. Some foreign goods have arrived, but it is difficult to open the market. Heavy 荆 oil is at $16 per 砠 (bushel) based on foreign standards, but traders are not eager to buy. Offered prices are $16.20-16.30 for heavy 荆 oil with wood, $16 for oil without wood, $15.30-15.40 for plain 荆 oil, and slightly over $15 for Macheng oil. However, prices have fallen to the bottom, and further declines are unlikely. However, soap factories have no use for it, and sales rely solely on candle making, which is limited. Therefore, observing the current inventory, even if the old oil is sold out before the new crop arrives, the new oil may not see strong sales. But because candle factories everywhere are actively using up their inventory, they will need to buy when the new crop arrives. Therefore, the sales market may become active after the new crop arrives.

Metals

New Arrivals of Thin Galvanized Iron Sheet

Due to previous shortages of thin galvanized iron sheet, various traders were actively purchasing, leading to a very good market. Standard prices were soaring, such as $1.45-1.46 per sheet for 3-foot 7-inch sheets, $1.25 per sheet for 3-foot 6-inch sheets, and $1.50 per sheet for 48-sheet American goods. However, eager buyers depleted market inventories, disappointing later purchasers. Recently, new arrivals of over 20,000 sheets, including British and Japanese goods, have been reported. Upon hearing this news, buyers have been actively purchasing. It is said that two or three thousand sheets have already been sold yesterday, and many construction traders are still negotiating, so market prices have not declined yet.

Spot Supplies of Tobacco Tinplate Exhausted

The recent purchases of tobacco tinplate by Tianjin tobacco and 青 traders have been favorable, so arriving goods have been nearly completely purchased. Standard prices have opened to $11.45 per bundle, and spot supplies in the market have been exhausted, so most traders are offering forward contracts. Yesterday was a weekday, but still hundreds of bundles were sold. Contracts for goods arriving by the end of this month opened at $11, goods arriving in the first ten days of next month opened at $10.06, and goods arriving in the second half of the month are estimated at $10.02. The most purchased contracts are for goods arriving this month.

Silk and Tea

Fleeting Sales of French Silk

Yesterday, French firm Credit Lyonnais reported that the Lyon raw silk market remained quiet. However, Chinese silk prices have risen sharply due to the rapid depreciation of the French exchange rate. In the past two days, the market price for white factory and Jing factory brand grades has increased to over $560 (Chinese currency) per bale, and the 三跳舞 (Three Dances) brand grade to over $520, a sharp increase of $40-50 compared to the beginning of the week. Yesterday, the French mail ship Ile de France exported only 274 pieces of yellow and white silk from firms such as Credit Lyonnais and Da Chang to Marseilles. The sales of French silk are fleeting.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essays

The Exercise of Wrist Power

— Ju Sheng

The employment of wrist power is a principle that everyone in the present day must know and master. For the sake of eating, needless to say, everyone must employ their flexible wrist power in order to achieve perpetual victory in the world of the "rice struggle". Those who do not know how to employ wrist power are behind the times, they are 'foolish'!

In fact, wrist power is not only employed for the sake of eating. Because with the flexibility of wrist power, after having a full meal, people still cannot forget it, in the hope of obtaining other things besides food. However, the situation is seen more truly and clearly in terms of eating.

A small clerk who earns thirty yuan a month is trembling with fear all day long, paying attention to the department head's expression, handling official matters perfectly to earn a word of praise or a smile of approval. On the one hand, he must employ wrist power to make the director, who is not compatible with the department head, see that he is loyal to the director... Those who have flexible wrist power can please both sides and keep their jobs. If you do things with conscience, you can only sit at home!

As for the director level, they are not at ease either. They must make their superiors see that they are loyal, and make their subordinates have the enthusiasm to support them, and they themselves want to gain some real benefits from it. Therefore, the employment of wrist power must be even more flexible. A person who is nominally real and praised by the masses must have wrist power that others cannot reach. The so-called genius is perhaps this kind of person.

For one's own sake, it is natural to employ wrist power. If you want to trap, squeeze out, or attack someone, you must also employ your wrist power! You must make them feel the bitterness of "a mute eating Coptis chinensis" invisibly, and you yourself are safe and sound, getting what you want! The so-called "killing without seeing blood", "killing without using a knife", is this. It is the employment of wrist power.

Fabricating facts, spreading rumors... are all ways to employ wrist power. However, everything is changing with each passing day, and everything is progressing. It can be seen that there are countless new ways to employ wrist power!

If you trust others too much, or you are too honest, that is by no means your advantage, but your weakness; if you cannot play a little wrist power, you are too "young and inexperienced"! Then you are 'foolish'! You are a fool!

The employment of wrist power is necessary in all situations. No matter who you are dealing with, no matter whether the other party is a great man who talks about beautiful terms, a student with a square hat who has studied abroad, a pioneer of the new era... when they are all Chinese, they will use wrist power to deal with you; if you do not know how to use it, are you not falling behind?

Learn! Learn from society! The employment of wrist power is necessary for us!

However, however,... ah! There is no need to turn around and say it, right?

Moonlit Night

— Qian Xu

The moon shines round and bright overhead.

The water ripples, and the reeds on the shore are blown by the wind in a rhythmic way. In the distance, the trees are dense and black, but their outlines are carved by the moonlight. The mountain peaks are crawling on the ground like lions, seemingly always raising their heads to exhale. It is so quiet that even the sound of barking dogs cannot be heard. This clear and pure moonlit night seems to fully tell us: "Autumn is truly great!"

We rowed a small boat and swayed on the lake. Apart from the sound of the oars and the water, we were all silent. Really, only in this way can we appreciate the taste of stillness.

We abandoned the boat and landed on the not-so-steep mountain peaks. At this time, overlooking the entire town, it was all in sight, but we could not see any lights or hear any subtle sounds. We were very happy. Some people let out a long howl, releasing the depression in their chests. Some people sang in a low voice, seemingly expressing a moment of joy. I looked around at my companions, and everyone had a proud look on their faces. Probably the usual worries, at this bright moon, have been washed away by the mountain scenery.

Time will not come again. In this beautiful and delightful time, everyone's forgetting themselves and cheering is not to be condemned. However, good times do not last long. When we discovered that Yi Ping was bowing her head in sorrow, we became bored again.

The reason is that Yi Ping chanted two lines of poetry: "The people who came to enjoy the moon together, where are they now? The scenery seems to be the same as last year." It turned out that compared to last year's Mid-Autumn Festival, there were three or four fewer mountain companions who came together.

In a blink of an eye, this has become a three-year-old story.

Now I live in Shanghai. At this bright moon, although there are still one or two old companions with whom I can talk, the scenery is no longer the same, so what fun is there to speak of. Even more thinking of the old companions in the hometown, under the cool moonlight, swaying on the lake and mountains, checking the companions who are as rare as morning stars, and then reciting the old poems chanted by Yi Ping, I am afraid that not only will there be a lack of interest, but also a sadness that wants to be cut off.

Gathering has no fixed time, and the whip of life is always driving us, so why should we be sad and mournful.

Let him bury himself deep in our hearts, my friends, never remember again.

We really need to embark on a new path.

Imagining a Portrait of Someone After a Breakup

Autumn Harvest

— Yi

The small red door of Old Master Li's new house opened, and Wang the Old Man walked out with a mournful face. Judging from his dejected look, his request to Old Master Li had again been denied. Since the beginning of autumn, Wang the Old Man had walked out of this small red door more than ten times, each time with a more sorrowful expression.

"Old Man Wang, how is it? Still nothing?"

Standing in front of the opposite Japanese-style house, the mother of Li Sanzi asked with concern.

"Sister-in-law, don't mention it. In this year, really, how am I supposed to live?"

Wang the Old Man replied dejectedly, and then walked across the road. At this time, he was thinking, "The Li Sister-in-law's family must have something to eat!" But as he approached the Li Sister-in-law, he noticed that her face was different from a few days ago. A few nights ago, after failing to borrow rice from Old Master Li's house, he had come to her house for a meal. At that time, she and her son seemed very happy, talking and laughing to comfort him. But today was different. The Li Sister-in-law's face seemed to have just been crying, with streaks of tears, and her eyes were swollen and unfocused. He thought, "Are they like me too?"

"Li Sister-in-law, where is Brother Sanzi? Is he still doing business in the city?"

When the Li Sister-in-law heard her son's name, tears fell from her eyes. Wang the Old Man was immediately stunned. He couldn't figure it out for a moment and didn't know what to say to comfort her.

"Old Man Wang, I'm really heartbroken! Just three days ago, he went to the city to do business and was arrested! Those damn devils, I don't know what wrongs I've committed in my previous life with them. He's a good son, Old Man Wang, you know, he's always been an honest and law-abiding child. But they said he was a rice-robbing criminal and should be imprisoned. Old Man Wang, you think, he's my only son, and I've been counting on him to support me for the rest of my life. But now those damn devils have arrested him. What am I supposed to do?"

The Li Sister-in-law spoke while crying, and by the end, she was sobbing uncontrollably. Wang the Old Man really didn't know what to say. He could only comfort her by saying:

"Ah! Li Sister-in-law, don't cry. Crying won't help. I think Heaven won't let good people suffer unjustly. A good child like Brother Sanzi, Heaven will eventually pity him. You should still go and ask Old Master Li to think of a way to save him. I think Old Master Li is your uncle, so he's closer to you than us. Surely he won't watch Brother Sanzi suffer unjustly in vain?"

"Ah! Old Man Wang, don't mention our old uncle. Rich people won't pity poor relatives. I've already looked for him, but not only did he not think of a way for me, but he also said that I spoiled my son, leading to this result today. What can I say?"

Page 19

?

"Hmm, there really are such heartless people in the world!"

Wang the Old Man sighed and lowered his head. His stomach, which hadn't eaten anything for two days, made him unable to endure it any longer. He said goodbye to the Li Sister-in-law and dragged his heavy legs towards the house of Master Ma in the West Village.

The autumn sun was gentle. On this vast plain, when it reached dusk, the purple light of the sun shone on the earth, and a golden picture was beautifully draped over the plain. Although the fields were full of withered rice straw and the decaying bushes scattered on the ridges, the barren land accentuated the golden beauty. Wang the Old Man walked out of the West Village dejectedly. He stared at the withered rice straw, lost in thought. The autumn harvest, for him, was a despair.

Women

— Yun

I do have a bit of a liking for peace and quiet. If the place I live has too many children, or if the people are too complicated or too noisy, it would be very difficult for me to live there for any length of time. Therefore, moving house is like a regular occurrence for me.

This new house I moved into is indeed very nice, and it’s also very quiet, as quiet as a Zen temple. There are no children in the house, and the third floor is still empty. I’ve been living here for two days, and what do the landlord and landlady look like? I have no idea at all. According to that young woman living in the back room on the third floor—who was the one who showed me the house when I first came to see it—the landlord runs a candy factory, and the landlady has to go to the factory with the landlord during the day, not returning until late at night. However, after living here for a short time, I began to have doubts about the young woman’s background.

This woman lives with her husband in a narrow back room on the third floor. Judging by her age, she couldn’t be more than twenty. Her appearance is quite pleasing: with a melon-seed-shaped face and a slender, graceful figure. But her home is very simple. Besides her husband, there’s also an elderly “Mama”—supposedly her own mother. Yet why does she willingly let her sleep under the staircase every night and work for them like a servant during the day? At first, I really couldn’t stand to watch it, and I felt a faint sense of indignation.

Her husband is a young fellow just like her, but he has no masculine spirit at all, hiding in his bedroom all day long, not even daring to step out of the front door.

Every day, as the sun sets, after having dinner, this young lady invariably dresses up in a gaudy manner, puts on rouge, and leaves her husband, looking charming and moving, to go out with her mother, not returning until the clock strikes two. “Where on earth does she go out to stroll? Doesn’t she get tired of strolling like this every night?” I couldn’t help thinking this as I heard her slow, weak, seemingly exhausted footsteps moving on the staircase.

But the young lady’s secret was finally discovered by me one day by chance.

That day at the Great World amusement park, I saw this young lady talking and flirting with a middle-aged man. Their attitude was so intimate, flirtatious, and gentle… Ha! Ha, this young lady, her secret has been completely discovered by me tonight. So, I no longer dared to pass in front of her, and I quickly left this dark place.

“Ah, this young lady—her youth and soul have been completely ravaged by the demons of this city.” As I returned, I couldn’t help sighing like this.

East, West, South, North

— Sanduo

Our national essence is “Everyone sweeps the snow from his own doorstep, and doesn’t care about the frost on his neighbor’s roof.” Although this antiquated saying cannot be applied to modern times, the fact that people are selling Japanese goods with a clear conscience is like a bomb. It’s just too unlike “All within the four seas are brothers.”

It’s natural to be young and impetuous. For the sake of a small matter, they fight until their eyes and noses are swollen. Not to mention that our bodies and hair are received from our parents, but sticking plasters on ourselves is ultimately a losing proposition and not worth it.

Striving for honor rather than wealth still has some reason to it. Spending a few dollars is ultimately a small matter, while the face gained can allow you to give a loud and satisfying thumb’s up for the rest of your life.

We have been shouting to boycott Japanese goods until we are exhausted. What can be done about the national tendency to grab bargains? If you want to love your country, then manufacture cheap domestic goods. Without a boycott, there will naturally be a boycott. Things like the kneeling-and-crying group, with their tears streaming down their faces, are simply laughable.

Love for one’s country should be in one’s heart. If you say you don’t buy Japanese goods and you haven’t bought Japanese goods, if you can do that, then without a boycott, there will naturally be a boycott. Why trouble yourself to throw bombs?

Nothing is more tragic than the death of the heart. Love your country as much as you want, but unscrupulous merchants will still be unscrupulous merchants. The front wave pushes the back wave, and Yue Lai succeeds Yue Lai. The example of Liu Chongwu is a warning.

Correction: In yesterday’s “East, West, South, North” article, the Shanghai Xingye Bank was incorrectly referred to as the “China” Xingye Bank. We hereby correct this.

Selling Articles and Signing Names

— Especially

Selling articles seems like a beautiful thing on the surface, but in reality, it involves many pains, especially for those who rely on writing to make a living. However, this fact is often overlooked because objective imagination is not reality, and the true situation can only be understood by oneself.

Selling articles, in the eyes of an objective observer, might be seen as “a thousand words at the desk, ready to be written,” and naturally, along with that, the rustling of silver dollars would also be “readily available.” This might happen, but it’s probably not very common.

Here, some people see the loveliness of the “rustling” and forget the pitifulness of the “desk work.” Thus, more people write articles. As a result, the “pitifulness” not only isn’t avoided, but instead increases, while the hope of “readily available” often doesn’t come true.

In order to compete, the need for “signing names” was discovered. Originally, signing names wasn’t a big deal, or it could be said that it didn’t have a very significant meaning. At most, it was just to conceal the reality of one’s real name for the convenience of writing.

Now, this seems to have become a trend. It’s very common and not surprising for one person to have more than one signature, even up to five or six. Because it’s not surprising, a signature that isn’t a big deal has been clouded by a kind of misfortune. It is not only invited by Zhang San to help out, but also has to entertain Li Si’s social occasions. If you’re not careful, Zhao Wu next door will also invite it to say a few words. Thus, it holds several positions and is extraordinarily prominent.

Naturally, prominence is a glorious thing. Since you’re “kindly not rejected,” it’s “good luck” shining upon you. This is something to be pleased about. There’s no need to register it at the trademark bureau, and there’s no need to be too stingy and claim it as private property. Because the name belongs to the public and should be used freely.

Shen Bao Architectural Weekly

A Record of the Completion of the World's Largest Submarine Tunnel

— Yan Ming

The Queen's Tunnel, which connects the two major cities of Liverpool and Birkenhead in England, is not only the world's largest submarine tunnel, but also one of the world's greatest engineering feats in recent times. Not long ago, the world's largest submarine tunnel was completed by the British Emperor and Empress, who came from London to Liverpool to attend the inauguration ceremony, presenting Liverpool with an unprecedented grand occasion. The construction of the tunnel, from the laying of the foundation stone to its recent completion, took more than eight years and cost a staggering £10 million. During the construction period, the government established a tunnel working committee to oversee the project. The tunnel working committee searched throughout the United Kingdom for all the famous engineering designers and architects, so that there was not a single engineering designer or architect in the country who was free to build the submarine tunnel, which shows the magnitude of the project, and truly opened a new era in the world's construction projects. The tunnel goes deep into the seabed, so that even the ships with the deepest draft in the world can pass over it without any obstruction. The tunnel is five miles long and about forty-four feet wide, and can accommodate four cars running parallel to each other at the same time. When this great project first started, despite the painstaking efforts of architects and engineering designers, many workers still sacrificed their lives inside. The cause of death was mostly due to the suffocation of air in the tunnel, which made it impossible to breathe. Because it is very difficult and impossible for the air to flow as smoothly as on the ground in a long and deep tunnel. But later, after long-term and meticulous research by the architects, they built three ventilation towers at each end of the tunnel to regulate the air inside and outside the tunnel. This project was done very perfectly, so people who pass through the tunnel now feel no different from being on the ground, and there is no feeling of suffocation at all.

Now, let me write down some of the scenes of the inauguration ceremony of the submarine tunnel at that time:

The inauguration ceremony was held in Liverpool on July 18 this year. That morning, the Emperor and Empress of England took a train from London to Liverpool to preside over the ceremony. The residents of Liverpool were overjoyed to meet this unprecedented event and were almost ecstatic. Wherever the Emperor and Empress passed, there was thunderous applause. People waved the national flag from the roofs and windows to express their warm welcome. Wang Street at the entrance of the tunnel was even more crowded with people, packed like sardines, waiting for the arrival of the Emperor and Empress. On both sides of the tunnel buildings, there were lively male and female elementary school students wearing colorful clothes, which attracted the attention of the Emperor and Empress. After the Emperor and Empress arrived in Liverpool by car, they changed to a car to Walton Park. The park was also completed at the same time as the submarine tunnel, and the Emperor took the opportunity to hold the completion ceremony. After the ceremony, they drove to Wang Street. When the crowd saw the Emperor and Empress driving to the street, they cheered in unison. It was almost noon, and the ceremony began. First, the Emperor inspected the army, and the Queen inspected the Red Cross Brigade in the Lancashire Army. After the inspection, the Mayor of Liverpool and Sir Witacre, Chairman of the Tunnel Working Committee, delivered welcome speeches in succession, followed by a speech by the Emperor, thanking the national construction workers and workers for their concerted efforts in completing this unique and magical project in the world. At the same time, he expressed his respect to those workers who died for their work. After the Emperor finished his speech, he pressed the button on the table in front of 150,000 people, and the curtain at the entrance of the tunnel automatically opened. The Emperor and Empress then took the car and set off for the tunnel first, led by the Liverpool Police Music Team. The car drove from the slope to the entrance of the tunnel, and they saw the words "Welcome Your Majesty" made of electric lights. Behind the Emperor's car, countless vehicles of nobles and civilians went one after another. Within an hour, a total of 2,500 vehicles had passed through.

What is regrettable is that, except for the opening ceremony day, the Liverpool City Government posted a notice that pedestrians are not allowed to pass through at ordinary times, except for those driving cars. This point is also the "fly in the ointment" after the completion of the world's largest submarine tunnel.

Architects in China

— Ya Jie

An architect is the only person who assists in making buildings stand tall and magnificent; modern skyscrapers and mansions have to go through the architect's preliminary design, construction supervision, post-construction arrangement, and constant advice. This is recognized by every Chinese person with a little common sense, but recently there has been a common phenomenon that there is a very strange understanding of the architectural engineering profession, that is, anti-architects are classified as upper-class, luxury, and people who diminish social production. This new concept is certainly due to the Chinese people's failure to thoroughly understand the detailed situation and specialized knowledge of the construction industry, resulting in a misunderstanding. At the same time, the professionals themselves cannot shirk their responsibility for neglecting their own business, or even being despised. This is certainly undeniable;

Originally, the rise and fall, size, importance, and influence of the construction industry on the increase or decrease in the number of architects are on the same line and are directly proportional. In other words, if a country needs a large number of buildings, strives to develop the construction industry, and vigorously seeks solutions to the people's livelihood, then the cultivation and recruitment of specialized personnel is inevitable. Otherwise, the result will be the opposite.

Reasoning from the perspective of architects serving the society and doing their best, it is impossible to equate them with general luxury goods, such as priceless treasures, expensive and gorgeous cars, and other goods purchased with large sums of money, or to further compare them, or to include them in the necessities of daily life, such as food, clothing, housing, and transportation, the four major elements of life, it does not seem inappropriate. Because the spirit of architectural engineering and the business of architects are both to serve society and benefit the people, and they will do their best to reduce the burden of the owners. Even if it has reached the minimum limit, they will try to find ways to avoid extra expenses. However, ordinary people not only do not understand this, but instead think that the cost is only more and not less. The lack of common sense and the unclear understanding are deeply regrettable.

However, the occurrence of things, as well as the beginning of rumors, must first have a cause and then a result. Then, the slander that architects are considered to be appendages of luxury assets must have a cause, and it is definitely not a baseless rumor. Therefore, in the future, Chinese architects should strive to make up for the aftermath, think of ways to reverse this kind of fallacy, and create another style, so that the Chinese people will have another new concept and new tendency.

Therefore, the reason why the advocacy of the above fallacy has not been extinguished to this day is that some professionals have neglected their business or have a lazy service spirit, resulting in this. If they can each broaden their horizons, not be concerned about the lack of profit in the entrusted business, or not focus their thoughts on the views of the great buildings being entrusted, then there are few individuals who will not succeed, and their status will not increase accordingly. How many people in the country can pay attention to this point? There are still people who can understand it more deeply, so that the reliability and cost-saving of architectural professional technology can penetrate the hearts of the people and be imported into the folk, so that they can thoroughly realize that the so-called lower-level work can be attractive and confusing. Try to compare the medical and architectural industries, which are the same specialized academic and sophisticated technologies. The former is universally recognized by the world and regarded as a necessity, while the latter is discriminated against and regarded as a luxury. Is the latter's academic technology slightly inferior to the former, or are there more patients and is it more important than building houses? One is that academic theories and skills penetrate the hearts of the people and are respected by the world, and the other is that the understanding is insufficient and the impression is shallower. The error in viewpoint leads to discrimination, and the evil thoughts in the necessary principles lead to loss of faith. I hope that the architects in our country should catch up quickly, so that the service purpose and benefits can be widely promoted, so that even peddlers and pawns in the folk can know its wonders, and they will believe in it for life. Naturally, the business will be inextricably linked with the public, and at the same time, the fallacy will be extinguished, the reputation will increase day by day, the career will flourish, and the status will increase invisibly.

Waterproofing for Buildings

— Long

Our country's architectural industry has been progressing rapidly in recent years. Engineering is becoming more grand, and designs are becoming more meticulous. Consequently, preventing water damage and dampness has also been recognized as an important issue. Dampness in buildings is not only detrimental to aesthetics but also unacceptable from a hygienic standpoint. In factories and warehouses, it can lead to rust in machinery and mold in goods. Furthermore, for buildings with underground pits or water towers, waterproofing is even more crucial.

Waterproofing may seem simple, but it is actually quite complex. The waterproofing methods for underground pits differ from those for walls, and the methods for roofs differ from those for water towers. For repairing underground pits, chemical substances are needed to make the cement solidify within seconds to withstand pressure of hundreds of pounds per square inch. Walls require transparent waterproofing materials that do not compromise the original aesthetics. Roofs need durable and resilient materials, while water towers require non-toxic materials. Since the materials vary, the methods also differ, requiring specialized study to understand.

Given the complexity of waterproofing types and methods, as described above, manufacturers of waterproofing materials must possess unique knowledge, extensive experience, more than ten exquisite products, and dozens of well-trained workers to meet the demands.

Dealers in building materials in Shanghai often lack a complete range of waterproofing materials and are not very clear about their usage, causing inconvenience to users. The Yale Manufacturing Factory has specialized research on waterproofing materials and projects, and is considered unparalleled in our country. To promote widespread knowledge of waterproofing engineering, the factory has published a booklet entitled "Building Waterproofing Methods" for reference by the construction industry. It has also established an engineering department to provide consultation and undertake various waterproofing and repair projects, greatly benefiting various sectors.

Japanese Paper Houses

— Yangyang

A Miracle in the Architectural World

Our eastern neighbor, the Yamato people, though standing among the world's first-class powers, seem to possess a national character of ingenuity and fickleness, which is perhaps not highly praised by the world. Their industrial manufacturing, especially for export goods, is particularly frivolous. Even in the realm of children's toys, they generally prioritize cost reduction and labor savings, aiming for quick profits. For a long time, our country has been their sole distribution point. Since the "September 18th" and "January 28th" incidents, the people of our country have awakened, on the one hand shouting for economic severance, and on the other hand earnestly creating domestic goods. From both active and passive perspectives, it seems that we truly possess a great spirit of striving for strength! However, what is the actual situation? We see reports of "reciprocal trade treaties" and continuous compromises. Considering the past abnormal state of being their "exclusive agent" and "sole distributor," we find that there is trade but perhaps no true reciprocity. This is an extremely contradictory matter, without any doubt! However, it must be said that the above discussion is all beside the point and has nothing to do with the main topic, so there's no need to dwell on it. Only the four words "ingenuity and extravagance" are relevant to the following brief account in this article.

In the Japanese architectural world, there is an architect named Kyo Gorō who invented a type of "paper house." Just imagine: building a house for people to live in entirely out of paper, how ingenious is that? And that a house can actually be made of paper, how changeable is that? This is not only a wonder of the world and a beautiful tale in the architectural circles of various countries, but also, in a country frequently plagued by earthquakes and typhoons, these paper houses can solve the housing problem and greatly avoid or reduce the degree of danger. Kyo Gorō's creative motivation originally arose from the hope of resisting earthquakes and typhoons, but whether his future endeavors will be successful remains uncertain. The architect is currently working hard to refine his designs without any discouragement. Therefore, people generally predict that this ingenious structure will be able to make new contributions to the architectural world and provide considerable benefits to the changeable people of that nation. As for our thoughts on disaster relief and helping our neighbors, we do not discriminate based on hatred. Therefore, we also deeply hope for its success, opening a new era in the architectural world. If it can be further promoted for practical use, then the people living in a country plagued by frequent typhoons and earthquakes can rely on these paper houses to protect their lives, which would indeed be a blessing for humanity.

The main material for building these paper houses is the best quality Manila paper weighing over 100 pounds. This paper is highly adhesive and the most durable in its class. Its length and width are also very large. The walls, roof, windows, and all important parts of the house are made by pasting this Manila paper together. However, the thickness of each part varies, with the number of layers ranging from several to dozens. Each layer of paper is coated with thick white glue, and the outermost layer is covered with fish oil. After prolonged shade drying, various beautiful patterns are added, making it resistant to wind and rain without peeling off. To prevent strong sunlight from scorching the fish oil and white glue, causing them to melt and lose their adhesion, which would result in the house collapsing and the skylights opening, a scientific method is used to create a chemical solution that resists sunlight and is applied to the roof and walls to prevent unforeseen circumstances. The supporting beams, door and window frames, and wall joints are all reinforced with extremely thin copper strips and iron hooks, the weight of which is minimized to prevent injury if they fall.

In the architect's overall plan, it is estimated that each fully completed paper house requires approximately 25,000 sheets of Manila paper, about 200 catties of fish oil and white glue combined, and about 140 pieces of thin steel strips and small iron hooks. The equipment is not very simple, and all necessary structures are included, not differing much from houses built with tiles and wood. Kyo Gorō is from Mooka Prefecture in Japan, a region surrounded by mountains and water, where earthquakes and typhoons are frequent, even during the pleasant days of spring and autumn. Living in constant fear for his safety, Kyo became deeply resentful. Therefore, he devoted himself to research for more than a decade, leading to the initial completion of the project. Furthermore, the entire house can be disassembled and assembled anywhere at any time. In other words, it can be moved and carried without any hindrance. It can also be called a traveling house.
